<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыжок.html>прыжо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pryžók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыжок.html>прыжка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыжок.html>прыжки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыжок.html>прыжко́в</a></b>)

<li>dive</li></ol>

***прыскать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прыскать.html>пры́скать</a> (29858)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pryskati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыскать.html>пры́скать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prýskatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыснуть.html>пры́снуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">попры́скать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to burst into laughter</li>
<li>to dart, to dash</li>
<li>to sprinkle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drizzle, to fall in small drops <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of rain</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***прыснуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прыснуть.html>пры́снуть</a> (14831)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пры́с(кать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prýs(katʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыснуть.html>пры́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prýsnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыскать.html>пры́скать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to burst into laughter</li>
<li>to dart, to dash</li>
<li>to sprinkle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gush, to spurt</li></ol>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пряжа.html>пря́жа</a> (31599)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pręďa</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:пряжа.html>пря́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjáža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прямик.html>прями́к</a> (10380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ík</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямик.html>прями́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjamík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямик.html>прямика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямик.html>прямики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямик.html>прямико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> straight path</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> direct, frank person</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямо.html>пря́мо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjámo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>straight</li>
<li>openly, blankly, frankly</li>
<li>real, really, truly</li>
<li>exactly, downright</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямо.html>пря́мо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjámo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***прямой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a> (951)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">прямъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straight, correct, honest, simple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjamój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пряме́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пряме́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пряме́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>straight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>у́гол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prjamój úgol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">right angle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>direct</li>
<li>straightforward</li>
<li>through <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a train</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>downright</li>
<li>outspoken, frank</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjamój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>пряма́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">dative singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>пряма́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">instrumental singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>пряма́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">prepositional singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>пряма́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пря.html>пря</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мо́й</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1b/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>пряме́е, пряме́й, попряме́е, попряме́й</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-прям-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ой</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямолинейный.html>прямолине́йный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamolinéjnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямолинейность.html>прямолине́йность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjamolinéjnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямолинейность.html>прямолине́йности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямолинейность.html>прямолине́йности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямолинейность.html>прямолине́йностей</a></b>)

<ol><li>straightness, rectilinearity</li>
<li>straightforwardness, frankness <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a way that lacks sensitivity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>у́гол</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">úgol</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">angle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямоугольный.html>прямоуго́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjamougólʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>right-angled
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прямоугольный.html>прямоуго́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:треугольник.html>треуго́льник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prjamougólʹnyj</b> treugólʹnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">right-angled triangle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>rectangular</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пряный.html>пря́ный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjányj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***пряный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пряный.html>пря́ный</a> (16935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пьпьрѧнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pĭpĭręnŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peppery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пьпьръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pĭpĭrŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pepper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-ѧнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ęnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пряный.html>пря́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjányj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>spicy (containing spice)</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-прян-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прясть.html>прясть</a> (31811)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pręsti</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прясть.html>прясть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prjastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">спрясть</b>)

***псина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:псина.html>пси́на</a> (21452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:псина.html>пси́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">psína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:псина.html>пси́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:псина.html>пси́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:псина.html>пси́н</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пси́нка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dogmeat, dog flesh</li>
<li>smell of a dog, doggy odor</li>
<li>dog</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>пси́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> согласовываться <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>), 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>запах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плоть.html>плоть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ки</a></i> мн. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> употребимо.
</p>
